<div class="inner">

	<h3 class="large">How it works:</h3>
	<h2 class="large">The Union Plus Promise</h2>

	<section class="numbers-wrapper">

			<div class="number-item">
				<div class="number">
					<img src="/assets/images/1.svg">
				</div>

				<div class="text">
					<p class="big">Solidarity</p>

<p>We stand&nbsp;union-strong with the 13+ million union members to negotiate exclusive programs and prices.</p>


				</div>

			</div>
			<div class="number-item">
				<div class="number">
					<img src="/assets/images/2.svg">
				</div>

				<div class="text">
					<p class="big">Unique Benefits and Savings</p>

<p>If you're a union family, your unique benefits and savings can be accessed today,&nbsp;including discounts on AT&amp;T, travel, entertainment, hardship help grants and scholarships. No Union Plus membership required!</p>


				</div>

			</div>
			<div class="number-item">
				<div class="number">
					<img src="/assets/images/3.svg">
				</div>

				<div class="text">
					<p class="big">Social Responsibility</p>

<p class="big">Union Plus is a non-profit created&nbsp;by the AFL-CIO thirty&nbsp;years ago.&nbsp;When you use Union Plus benefits, you're supporting the labor movement — ensuring that you and your fellow union members remain union-strong for generations to come!</p>


				</div>

			</div>

	</section>
